7a8(mdo 'grel): 'phrul dga' rnams su'o// de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas dga' ldan rnams su'o// de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni 'thab bral ba rnams su'o// de bas ches shas chung bad 
7b1(mdo 'grel): debs ches yang bas ni sum cu rtsag sum pa rnams su'o// debs ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams sur// de bsachas shas rdung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni ma rnams 
7b2(mdo 'grel): dang skal ba mnyam par skye bar 'gyur ro// ji ste mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skyen yang srog gcod pa spong bas ni tshe ring por 'gyur ro// ma byin par len pa spong bas ni longs spyod chen por 'gyur ro// 'dod pa log 
7b3(mdo 'grel): par g.yem pa spong bas ni chung ma 'gran zla med par 'gyur ro// brdzun du smra ba spong bas ni skur ba mang bar mi 'gyur ro// phra ma 'thong bas ni mdza' bo dang 'bye bar mi 'gyur ro// tshig rtsub po spong bas ni yid du mi 'ong ba'i sgra 
7b4(mdo 'grel): thos par mi 'gyur ro// tshig 'khyal pa spong bas ni tshig mnyan par 'gyur ro// chags sems med pas ni 'dod chags che bar mi 'gyur ro// gnod sems med pas ni zhe sdang che bar mi 'gyur ro// yang dag pa'i lta bas ni 
7b5(mdo 'grel): gti mug che bar mi 'gyur ro// sems can dmyal bar myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba ched rje matsa'i tshad bskal par len pa 'di mchog yin 
7b6(mdo 'grel): no// dud 'gro myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas sa srung gi bus sa srung gi bu nyid dang / rab tu brtan pas rab tu brtan pa nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no// yi dgas kyi skye gnas 
7b7(mdo 'grel): su skye bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas rgyal po gshin rje'i gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi sems can rnams kyi rgyal srid kyi dbang phyug la dbang byed de 'di ni mchog yin no// mi'i skye gnas 
7b8(mdo 'grel): myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pa sang las nus las nus nyid du thob pa 'di mchog yin no// rgyal chen bzhi'i ris myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par 
8a1(mdo 'grel): smin pas rgyal po chen po bzhi rnams rgyal srid kyi dbang phyug la dbang byed pa 'di mchog yin no// sum cu rtsa gsum myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi// / 
8a2(mdo 'grel): rnam par smin pa brgya byin gyis brgya byin nyid thob pa mchog yin no// 'thab bral myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas rab 'thab bral gyis rab 'thab bral nyid thob pa 
8a3(mdo 'grel): 'di mchog yin no// dga' ldan myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas yongs su dga' ldan gyis yongs su dga' ldan nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no// 'phrul dga' byor
8a4(mdo 'grel): bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gis rnam par smin pas rab sprul gyis rab sprul nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no// gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las
8a5(mdo 'grel): gang gi rnam par smin pas dbang byed kyis dbang byed nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams bkres pa dang / skom pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams dang / nub kyi ba 
8a6(mdo 'grel): lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams
8a7(mdo 'grel): dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang yod do// de yan chad la ni bkres pa dang / skom pa med do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la kha zas 'di lta ste/ 'bras chan dang / zan dang 
8a8(mdo 'grel): phye dang / sha dang / rus pa rnams yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod la yang yod do// byang gi sgram snyan gyi mi rnams ni ma rmos ma btab pa'i 'bras sA lu'i 'bru ba'o// 
8b1(mdo 'grel): rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams ni dri za'i zas dang bdud rtsi'i zas za'o// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa
8b2(mdo 'grel): rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no// de yan chad la ni kham gyi zas med do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi bdud rtsi ni rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon pa 
8b3(mdo 'grel): dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams so// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dka' 
8b4(mdo 'grel): ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams dang de bzhin no// tshangs ris pa rnams la ni med do// de yan chad la yang med do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la bshang ba dang gci ba yod pa bzhin du shar
8b5(mdo 'grel): gyi lus 'phags po rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams la yang yod do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do// de yan chad la yang med do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi/ 
8b6(mdo 'grel): mi rnams la char 'bab mkhas pa dang / char 'bab mi mkhas pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen 
8b7(mdo 'grel): bzhi'i rnams la ni med do// de yan chad la yang med do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la lo legs pa dang / mu ge yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod
8b8(mdo 'grel): do// byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do// de yan chad la yang med do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la 'jigs pa dang / bde ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 
9a1(mdo 'grel): 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang smon pa rnams la yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la ni med do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams 
9a2(mdo 'grel): dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yod do// tshangs ris pa rnams la ni med do// de yan chad la yang med do// 
9a3(mdo 'grel): 'jig rten bzhag pa las tshigs gsum pa'o// // mdo la/ nyo tshong mdog dang khang pa dang / gding ba dang ni bzhag gos dang // yang brdul rab sgre ba dang // tha dad pag ma len dang bcu// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling
9a4(mdo 'grel): gi mi rnams la nor ram/ 'bru 'am/ gser ram dngul nyo tshar bya ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams dang / rgyal chen 
9a5(mdo 'grel): bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do// de yan chad la yang med do// 'di snyam du/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams ni nor dang 'bru rnams kyis nyo tshong byed do// shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams ni ras dang be'u ras rnams kyis
9a6(mdo 'grel): so// rab kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams ni ba lang dang ner bu rnams kyis so zhes zer ba yod do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi mdog nag po dang // dkar po dang / sngo bsangs dang / mdog skya snar rnam pa bzhi 
9a7(mdo 'grel): yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams kyang de bzhin no// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni mdog gcig pa ste dkar po'o// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi mdog
9a8(mdo 'grel): ni rnam pa bzhi'o// sngon po dang / ser po dang / dkar po dang / dmar po rnams so// rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang 
9b1(mdo 'grel): dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyang de bzhin no// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams dang mdog gcig pa ste dkar po'o// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ji lta/ 
9b2(mdo 'grel): bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba 
9b3(mdo 'grel): rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / 
9b4(mdo 'grel): shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no// nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched dang / rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched dang / ci yang med pa'i phyir skye mched dang / 'du shes med 'du 
9b5(mdo 'grel): shes med min skye mched la ni kha dog med do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi khang pa ched du byas pa dang / ched du byas pa ma yin pa dang / khang bzangs dang / sa khang rnams yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 
9b6(mdo 'grel): 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams kyi khang pa ni ched du byas pa ma yin pa'i sa khang ngo // rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams kyi gzhal med khang ni ched du/ 
9b7(mdo 'grel): byas pa dang ched du byas pa ma yin pa'o// rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha rnams kyi 'jig rten pa bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang // 
9b8(mdo 'grel): gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no// tshangs ris pa rnams kyis gzhal med khang rnams ni ched du byas pa ma yin pa'o// tshangs ris pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i 'dun na 'don pa dang / 
10a1(mdo 'grel): tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dag rgyas pa
10a2(mdo 'grel): rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min// 
10a3(mdo 'grel): pa rnams kyi gzhal med khang yang ched du byas pa ma yin no// gzugs med pa rnams la ni khang pa med pa'o// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la gding ba dang bgo ba 'di lta ste/ bal gos dang / sha na'i ras dang / 
10a4(mdo 'grel): gso ma'i ras dang / zar ma'i ras dang / ras gos dang / zab dar dang / go tam pa'i ras dang / rtswa du ko la'i gos dang / a pa ran+ti ka'i gos dang / ras dang / be'u ras yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags 
10a5(mdo 'grel): pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos gyon no// ji ltar byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams dpag bsam shing las byung 
10a6(mdo 'grel): ba'i gos gyon pa bzhin du rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / subacu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha 
10a7(mdo 'grel): rnams kyang de bzhin no// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ni gos gyon bzhin du skye'o// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams/ 
10a8(mdo 'grel): dang / tshad med 'ong ba rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang 
10b1(mdo 'grel): 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de gos gyon bzhin du skye'o// 
10b2(mdo 'grel): byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams kyi dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos kyi shing ni rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams so// bzhag gos rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon pa 
10b3(mdo 'grel): dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams so// dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams so// dpag 
10b4(mdo 'grel): bsam shing las byung ba'i gos ji lta bu 'dod pa de lta bu skyes pa'am/ bud med dag gis sems bskyed ma thag tu de la yal ga 'dud par byed do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi dpag bsam shing las byA/ 
10b5(mdo 'grel): ba'i gos kyi shing rnams kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams so// bzhag gos kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar ba dang / dkar po rnams// / 
10b6(mdo 'grel): se// dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams te// dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos ji lta bu 'dod pa de lta bu lha'i bu 'am/ 
10b7(mdo 'grel): lha'i bu mo dag gi sems bskyed ma thag tu yal ga gdud par byed de/ de'i lag tu 'ong bar 'gyur ro// rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' 
10b8(mdo 'grel): ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos med do// de yan chad la yang med// 
11a1(mdo 'grel): ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la gdide pa dang / bgo ba lci ba dang / yang ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams 
11a2(mdo 'grel): la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams kyi dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos la srang gcig yod do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi ni srad phyed do// sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi ni srang 
11a3(mdo 'grel): gi bzhi cha gcig go/ 'thab bral ba rnams kyi ni srang gang gi brgyad cha gcig go/ dga' ldan pa rnams kyi ni srang gi bcu drug cha gcig go/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams kyi sum cu rtsa gnyis kyi srang gi cha gcig 
11a4(mdo 'grel): go/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi dpag bsam gyi shing las byung ba'i gos ni srang gi drug cu rtsa bzhi'i cha gcig las med do// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams kyi ni gzhal du med pa'i gos yin no// 
11a5(mdo 'grel): tshangs ris pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i 'dun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba 
11a6(mdo 'grel): rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang // 
11a7(mdo 'grel): gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min lha rnams kyi yang gzhal du med pa'i gos yin no// nyi zer gyi rdul bzhi bcu rtsa dgu'i cha gcig ni rdul phra rab yin no// rdul phra rab 
11a8(mdo 'grel): bdun ni rdul phra mo gcig go/ rdul phra mo bdun la ni nyi zer gyi rdul gcig go/ nyi zer gyi rdul bdun la ni ri bong gi rdul gcig go/ ri bong gi rdul bdun la ni lug rdul gcig go/ lug rdul bdun la ni 
11b1(mdo 'grel): glang rdul gcig go/ glang rdul bdun la ni sro ma gcig go/ sro ma bdun la ni a ba ga na gcig go/ a ba ga na gcig la ni ba ti ka gcig go/ ba ti ka bdun la ni nas 'bru gcig go/ nas 'bru 
11b2(mdo 'grel): bdun la ni sor gcig go/ sor nyi shu rtsa bzhi la ni khru gang ngo // 'dzam bu'i gi mi rnams kha cig ni khru tshad de ltar brtsis pa'i khru phyed dang bzhi pa'o// kha cig ni khru bzhi pa'o// shar gyi lus 'phags pa 
11b3(mdo 'grel): rnams ni khru brgyad pa'o// nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams ni khru bcu drug pa'o// byang gi sgra mi sman gyi mi rnams ni khru sum cu rtsa gnyis pa'o// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi lus thob pa ni rgyang grags kyi bzhi 
11b4(mdo 'grel): cha gcig gi/ sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams kyi ni rgyang grags kyi phyed do// 'thab bral ba rnams kyi ni rlung grags kyi bzhirtsa gsum mo// dga' ldan pa rnams kyi ni rgyang grags gcig go/ 'phrul dga' ba
11b5(mdo 'grel): rnams rgyang grags gcig dang / rgyang grags kyi bzhi cha gcig go/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed rnams kyi ni rgyang grags phyed dang gnyis so// tshangs ris pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad byed do// tshangs pa bdan na 'don
11b6(mdo 'grel): pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad gcig go/ tshangs pa chen po pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis so// 'od chung ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad gnyis so// tshad med 'od pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad bzhi'o// 'od gsal 
11b7(mdo 'grel): ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad brgyad do// dge chung ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad bcu drug go/ tshad med dge ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad sum cu rtsa gnyis so// dag rgyas pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad drug cu rtsa bzhi'o// 
11b8(mdo 'grel): sprin med pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga'o// bsod nams skyes pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu'o// 'bras bu che ba'i lha rnams kyi ni dpag tshad lnga brgya'o// 'du shes med pa'i 
12a1(mdo 'grel): sems can rnams kyi yang de dang 'dra'o// mi che ba'i lus thob pa ni dpag tshad stong ngo // mi gdung ba rnams kyi dpag tshad nyis stong ngo // gyen pa snang ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad bzhi 
12a2(mdo 'grel): stong ngo // shin du mthong ba pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad brgyad stong ngo // 'og min gyi lha rnams kyi lus thob pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad khri drug stong ngo // gzugs med pa rnams la ni bsags pa'i lus med do// 
12a3(mdo 'grel): nyi zer gyi rdul bzhi bcu rtsa dgu'i cha gcig gi ni rdul phra rab yin no// rdul phra rab bdud la ni rdul phra lo gcig go/ rdul phra mo bdun la ni nyi zer gyi rdul gcig go/ nyi zer gyi rdul bdun la ni ri bong gi rdul gcig/ 
12a4(mdo 'grel): ri bong gi rdul bdun la ni lug rdul gcig go/ lug rdul bdun la ni glang rdul gcig go/ glang rdul bdun la ni sro ma gcig go/ sro ma bdun la ni a ba ga na gcig go/ a ba ga na bdun la ni ba ti ka 
12a5(mdo 'grel): gcig go/ ba ti ka bdun la na nas 'bru gcig go/ nas 'bru bdun la ni sor gcig go/ sor nyi shu rtsa bzhi la khrukhu gang ngo // 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kha cig gos khru tshad 'di lta bur brtsis pa'i khru brgyad pa// 
12a6(mdo 'grel): gyon no// kha tsag ni khru bcu pa'o// shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams kyi khru nyi shu pa'o// nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams kyi ni khru bzhi bcu pa'o// byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams kyi ni dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i/ 
12a7(mdo 'grel): gas khru brgyad nupa gyon gyod do// rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha rnams kyang lus la ci ngan pa'i gos gyon no// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba 
12a8(mdo 'grel): rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams dang / tshangs ris pa rnams dang / tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa 
12b1(mdo 'grel): rnams dang / 'od rung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge rung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang // 
12b2(mdo 'grel): bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gyuro pa snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min pa rnams kyi yang de 
12b3(mdo 'grel): bzhin no// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams dbang po tha dad do// kha cig la ni mo'i dbang po dang / kha cig la ni pi'i dbang po yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa/ 
12b4(mdo 'grel): rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal cher bzhi pa'i lharnapas dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams 
12b5(mdo 'grel): dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang yod do// tshangs ris kyi rnams la ni mo'i dbang po yang med do// po'i dbang po yang med do// tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin du/ tshangs pa'i 
12b6(mdo 'grel): mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnabs dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge 
12b7(mdo 'grel): rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu 
12b8(mdo 'grel): mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la bag ma gtong ba dang / bag ma len pa yod pa bzhin du/ shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / 
13a1(mdo 'grel): rab kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la ni med do// rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral 
13a2(mdo 'grel): ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang yod do// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni bag ma gtong ba yang med len pa yang med do// / 
13a3(mdo 'grel): tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / 
13a4(mdo 'grel): dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba 
13a5(mdo 'grel): rnams dang / na pa snang brnams dang // natham thang ba rnams dang / legasan gyi spyarnams la yang bzhi // 'jig da gagasas pa tshigs pazhi pa'o// jig rted bzhag pa// 
13a6(mdo 'grel): bam po gnyis pa/ mdo la/ grang dang tsha dang dus tshigs mtshan mo dang / pha ma dang ni rje khol dang // nor dang 'bru dang mngon par zhen// bcu tshan yongs su brjod pa yin// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi 
13a7(mdo 'grel): mi rnams la shin tu grang ba dang / shin tu tsha ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams la ni med do// rgyal chen bzhi'i 
13a8(mdo 'grel): lha rnams la yang med do// de yan chad la yang med do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la dus tshigs 'di lta ste/ dgun dang / dpyid dang / dbyar yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams/ 
13b1(mdo 'grel): dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 
13b2(mdo 'grel): 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams la yang yod do// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni dus tshigs med do// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i 
13b3(mdo 'grel): mdun na 'dod pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'ong ba rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang // 
13b4(mdo 'grel): dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin du mthong 
13b5(mdo 'grel): ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la mtshan mo dang / nyin po yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa

13b7(mdo 'grel): gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams la yang yod do// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni mtshan mo yang med/ nyin mo yang med do// tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang // 
13b8(mdo 'grel): tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med 
14a1(mdo 'grel): pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / myi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu//

14a6(mdo 'grel): bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de/

14a8(mdo 'grel): zan kyang yod do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni rje bo dang bran kyang yod do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams 
14b1(mdo 'grel): dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang de bzhin no// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni rje bo yang med bran yang med do// tshangs ris pa rnams la ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs
14b2(mdo 'grel): pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang // /

14b6(mdo 'grel): cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang de bzhin no// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni
14b7(mdo 'grel): nor yang med 'bru yang med do// tshangs ris kyi lha ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od rung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal 
14b8(mdo 'grel): ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / 
15a1(mdo 'grel): mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la pa 'am/ 
15a2(mdo 'grel): ma'am/ bu pho 'am bu mo 'am/ rje bo 'am/ bran nam/ nor ram/ 'bru la mngon par zhen pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do//

15a4(mdo 'grel): cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la yang

15a7(mdo 'grel): rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no// 'jig rten bzhag pa la so tshigs lnga pa'o// // mdo la/ zla mtshan 'khrig dang khu chu 
15a8(mdo 'grel): dang // tshe bsgyur dang ni chu klung brag/ sa la rdzing bu glang po dang // srungs ma 'khor los sgyur ba'i lam// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la bud med zla mtshan can dang / sbrum ma dang / bu btsa' ba yod 
15b1(mdo 'grel): babazhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / rub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyad pa rnams la yang yod do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi ni 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi khye'u 
15b2(mdo 'grel): 'am/ bu mo lo lnga len pa ji tsam pa de bzhin no// lha 'am lha'i bu mo'i 'phrag pa 'am phang bar sems can brdzus te skye bar 'gyur te/ de la lha 'am lha'i bu mo dag 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag gi bu'am bu mo snyam du 
15b3(mdo 'grel): sems so// khye'u dang bu mo de dag kyang 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag cag gi ma 'am pha'o snyam du sems so// sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams kyi ni lo drug lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no// 'thab bral ba rnams kyi ni 
15b4(mdo 'grel): lo bdun lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no// dga' ldan pa rnams kyi ni lo brgyad lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no// 'phrul dga' ba rnams kyi ni lo dgu lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no// gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi ni 'jam 
15b5(mdo 'grel): bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi khye'u dang bu mo lo bcu lon pa ji tsam pa de bzhin du lha 'am lha'i bu mo'i phrag pa'am phang bar brdzus te skye ba'i sems can 'byung bar 'gyur te/ de na lha 'am lha'i bu mo dag 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag 
15b6(mdo 'grel): gi bu'am bu mo snyam du sems so// khye'u dang bu mo de dag kyang 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag cag gi ma 'am pha'o snyam du sems so// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ni thog ma nas lus kyi yan lag dang zhing lag thams cad 
15b7(mdo 'grel): rdzogs par skye zhing 'chi ba na yang de kho na nyid do// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'ad pa rnams 
15b8(mdo 'grel): dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu 
16a1(mdo 'grel): che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og yin pa rnams kyang de bzhin no// 
16a2(mdo 'grel): gzugs med pa rnams la ni lus kyi gzugs med de/ de bas na de dag gi skye ba yang mi mngon/ 'chi 'pho ba yang mi mngon do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams mi tshangs par spyod pa 'khrig 
16a3(mdo 'grel): ba'i chos bsten pa na gnyis kyis gnyis sbyor ba bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / rab kyi ba lang pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / sum cu// 
16a4(mdo 'grel): rtsa gsum pa rnams kyang de bzhin no// 'thab bral ba rnams ni 'khyud pa tsam gyis gdung ba zhi par 'gyur ro// dga' ldan pa rnams kyis ni lag pa nas bzung ba tsam gyis so// 'phrul dga' ba rnams 
16a5(mdo 'grel): kyis brgad pa tsam gyis so// gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi ni bltas pa tsam gyis gdung bzhi par 'gyur ro// tshangs ris pa rnams la ni 'dod chags med do// tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba
16a6(mdo 'grel): bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang

16b1(mdo 'grel): 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la yang de bzhin no// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi ni rlung 'byung ngo // rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta

16b6(mdo 'grel): dmyal ba'i sems can gyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa gcig ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// dud 'gro'i skye gnas su skyes pa'i sems can rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha'i skal pa gcig te/ bar 
16b7(mdo 'grel): mdor 'chi ba ni yod do// mi rnams kyi nyin zhag sum nu gang yin pa de ni yi dgas rnams kyi zhin gcig ste/ nyin zhag de sum nu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ yi dgas 
16b8(mdo 'grel): rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lo lnga brgya ste/ bar mdor 'chi ba ni yod do// de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo khri lnga stong yod do// shar gyi lus 'phags kyi mi rnams kyi tshe'i 
17a1(mdo 'grel): tshad kyi mtha' ni lo nyis brgya lnga bcu ste/ bar mdor 'chi ba ni yod do// nub kyi ba lang spyod kyi mi rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo lnga brgya ste/ bar mdor 'chi ba ni yod do// byang gi sgra 
17a2(mdo 'grel): mi spyan gyi mi rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' nilo skong ste/ bar mdor 'chi ba med do// ci phyir byang gi sgra mi skar gyi mi rnams ni bar mdor 'chi ba ni med ce na/ de dag la bdag gib med cing yongs su 
17a3(mdo 'grel): 'dzin pa med de/ tshe nges shing khyad par 'gro ba yin pas/ de'i phyir byang gi sgra mi snyan rnams la bar ma dor 'chi ba med do// 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la yar skye ba dang / mar 'gro ba pa yod de/ 'dzam 
17a4(mdo 'grel): bu'i gling gi mi rnams re 'ga' ni tshe dpag tu med par 'gyur la/ re 'ga' ni tshe la banu par 'gyur ro// mi rnams kyi tshe lo lnga bcu gang yin pa de ni// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go// nyin zhag de 
17a5(mdo 'grel): sum nul zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur rabartsis pa'i lha'i lo lnga brgya ste/ bar mdor 'chi ba ni yod do// de mi'i ltar brtsin la 
17a6(mdo 'grel): sa ya phrag dgu yod do// de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po yang sos kyi nyin zhag gcig go/ nyin zhag de sum nu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba yang sos kyi 
17a7(mdo 'grel): sems can rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni de lo lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba pa'i lo lnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag 'bum drug khri nyis stong yod do// 
17a8(mdo 'grel): mi rnams kyi lo brgya gang yin pa de ni sum cu rtsa gsum gyi zhin zhag gcig go/ nyin zhag de sum nul zla ba gcig / zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' 
17b1(mdo 'grel): ni de lta bur brtas pa'i lha'i lo stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag gsum dang / sa ya phrag drug yod do// de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po thig nag gi nyin

22b2(mdo 'grel): 'di lta ste/ glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa bsrung ba dang / sba ba dang / mdzes par bya ba'i phyir shing sA la'i phreng ba rim pa bdun po dag gi nang na kha nang du bltas shing 'khod do// shing sA la'i phreng ba dang po'i nang 
22b3(mdo 'grel): na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du bltas te 'khod do// gnyis pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o// gsum pa'i nang du 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o// bzhi pa'i nang du 
22b4(mdo 'grel): 'dug pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o// lnga pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o// drug pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o// bdun pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag 
22b5(mdo 'grel): kyang kha nang du bltas te 'khod do// gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa shing sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa nas rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab par 'gro ba na/ res 'ga' ni tha mal pa'i tshul gyis 'gro'o// 
22b6(mdo 'grel): res 'ga' ni 'di lta ste/ lha 'am lha'i bu rdzu 'phrul che zhing mthu che ba gang yang rung ba dang 'dra bar bdag nyid mngon par sprul nas glang po che de dag thams cad kyi nang na dbang che bar grags pa gang yin pa de nyid kyi 
22b7(mdo 'grel): mgo 'am/ rgyab tu zhon te bsil sman dang pheg rdob pa dag rgya cher byed cing 'gro'o// gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan brdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyis nang du zhugs nas rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur
22b8(mdo 'grel): spyod pa de'i tshe glang po che brgyad stong po de dag 'di lta ste/ glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa de bsrung ba dang / sba ba dang / mdzes par bya ba'i phyir rdzing bu dal gyi 'bab gyis/ mtha' kho ra khor yug nas bskor te 
23a1(mdo 'grel): kha nang du bltas shing 'khod do// gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa rdzi dbu dal gyis 'bab kyi nang nas rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyad nas phyir byung ba de'i tshe de'i nang na glang 
23a2(mdo 'grel): po che dbang che bar grags pa gang yin pa de rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyi nang du zhugs nas pad+ma'i rtsa ba rnams blangs te/ shin tu bkrus shing rab tu gshal nas glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa la 'bul lo// 
23a3(mdo 'grel): gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pas zos shing 'thungs te 'drangs par gyur pa de'i tshe glang po che gzhan brgyad stong po de dag kyang rdzing bu brgyad stong dag gi nang na rdzing bu re re zhugs nas rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spod
23a4(mdo 'grel): do// pad+ma'i rtsa bdag blangs nas shin nubakrus shing rab dra ba shal te za'o// sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi glang ba che'i rgyal po g.yul ngor spyad pa rab tu phan pa'i mthun detsam mo// sems can thams cad n-i 
23a5(mdo 'grel): sungs ma dang bcas shing bsrung ba dang / skyob pa dang sbed pa dang mi 'bral te/ sems can gang dbang chung bar grags shing bsod nams chung la/ gzi brjid chung ba de dag ni brgya phrag mang po dang / stong phrag mang po la gcig 
23a6(mdo 'grel): bsrung ste/ dper na ba lang ngam lug brgya phrag mang po dang stong phrag mang po la gcig sung ba de bzhin du/ sems can gang dbang chung bar grags shing bsod nams chung la/ gzi brjid chung ba de dag ni brgya phrag mang po dang // 
23a7(mdo 'grel): stong phrag mang po la gcig sung ngo // sems can gang dbang che bar grags shing bsod nams che ba gzi brjid che ba de dag gi ni brgya phrag mang po dang / stong phrag mang po dag gis gcig pu bsung ste/ dper na 'khor los
23a8(mdo 'grel): skur ba'i rgyal po'am/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la brgya phrag mang po dang / stong phrag mang po dag gis gcig pu bsrung ba de bzhin du sems can gang dbang che bar
23b1(mdo 'grel): grags shing bsod nams che la gzi brjid che ba de dag la brgya phrag mang po dang / stong phrag mang po dag gis gcig du bsrung ngo // 'dir smras pa/ ji ste sems can thams cad srung ma dang bcas shing bsrung ba dang /

23b7(mdo 'grel): kyi lam po che dang / srang dang / bzhi mdo dang / sum mdo dang / dri 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang / me tog gi phreng ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang / zod dgram pa'i gnas rnams dang / bdung ba 'tshong ba'i gnas/ 
23b8(mdo 'grel): rnams dang / rtag tu myos pa'i gnas rnams dang / gsod byed kyi gnas rnams na su zhig 'dug ces 'jig rten 'di thams cad myal te/ ci ste dag gis sbyin par tshor na ni de dag gnas mthon po la 'god do// / 
24a1(mdo 'grel): ji ste de dag gis skyen par ma tshor na ni de dag gnas dma' ba la 'god do// zla ba phyed kyi tshes bcu bzhi la ni rgyal po chen po bzhi po de dag gi bu rnams kyis lam po che dang //

27b1(mdo 'grel): dag dang ni// nam mkha' lding dang nyo tshang dang // grang ba dag ni lnga bar byas// dus tshigs kyang ni tha ma yin// 'jig rten bzhag pa las tshigs drug pa'o// mdo la/ srung ma lha'i grong khyer srang rnams
